   || sūtraprasthānam ||	|| sUtra-prasTAnam ||
   || anuvyākhyānam ||	|| anuvyAKyAnam ||
   nārāyaṇaṃ nikhilapūrṇaguṇaikadehaṃ nirdoṣamāpyatamamapyakhilaiḥ suvākyaiḥ	nArAyaNam niKila-pUrNa-guNa-eka-deham nirdozam-Apyatamam-api-aKilEH su-vAkyEH
   asyodbhavādidamaśeṣaviśeṣato 'pi vandyaṃ sadā priyatamaṃ mama sannamāmi //	asya-udBavAt-idam-aSeza-viSezataH api vandyam sadA priyatamam mama sat-namAmi //
   MAnuv_1,1.1 //	Ma-anuv_1,1.1 //
   tameva śāstraprabhavaṃ praṇamya jagadgurūṇāṃ gurumañjasaiva /	tam-eva SAstra-praBavam praNamya jagadgurUNAm gurum-aQjasA-eva /
   viśeṣato me paramākhyavidyāvyākhyāṃ karomyanvapi cāhameva // MAnuv_1,1.2	viSezataH me parama-AKya-vidyA-vyAKyAm karomi-anu-api ca-aham-eva // Ma-anuv_1,1.2
   prādurbhūto harirvyāso viriñcabhavapūrvakaiḥ /	prAdurBUtaH hariH-vyAsaH viriQca-Bava-pUrvakEH /
   arthitaḥ paravidyākhyaṃ cakre śāstramanuttamam // MAnuv_1,1.3 //	arTitaH paravidyA-AKyam cakre SAstram-anuttamam // Ma-anuv_1,1.3 //
   gururgurūṇāṃ prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇāṃ bādarāyaṇaḥ /	guruH-gurUNAm praBavaH SAstrANAm bAdarAyaNaH /
   yatastaduditaṃ mānamajādibhyastadarthataḥ // MAnuv_1,1.4 //	yatas-tat-uditam mAnam-aja-AdiByaH-tad-arTataH // Ma-anuv_1,1.4 //
   vaktṛśrotṛprasaktīnāṃ yadāptiranukūlatā /	vaktR-SrotR-prasaktInAm yat-A-AptiH-anukUla-tA /
   āptavākyatayā tena śrutimūlatayā tathā // MAnuv_1,1.5 //	Apta-vAkya-tayA tena Sruti-mUla-tayA taTA // Ma-anuv_1,1.5 //
   yuktimūlatayā caiva prāmāṇyaṃ trividhaṃ mahat /	yukti-mUla-tayA ca-eva prAmANyam triviDam mahat /
   dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇāmekadhānyatra sarvaśaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.6 //	dRSyate brahmasUtrANAm-ekaDA-anyatra sarvaSas // Ma-anuv_1,1.6 //
   ato naitādṛśaṃ kiñcit pramāṇatamamiṣyate /	atas na-etAdRSam kiQcid pramANatamam-izyate /
   svayaṃ kṛtāpi tadvayākhyā kriyate spaṣṭatārthataḥ // MAnuv_1,1.7 //	svayam kRtA-api tadvayA-AKyA kriyate spazwatA-arTataH // Ma-anuv_1,1.7 //
   tatra tārāthamūlatvaṃ sarvaśaśastrasya ceṣyate /	tatra tArATa-mUla-tvam sarva-Sas-astrasya ca-izyate /
   sarvatrānugatatvena pṛthagoṅkriyate 'khilaiḥ // MAnuv_1,1.8 //	sarvatra-anugata-tvena pRTak-oFkriyate aKilEH // Ma-anuv_1,1.8 //
   otatvavācī hyoṅkāro vaktayasau tadguṇotatām /	otatva-vAcI hi-oFkAraH vaktayasO tad-guNa-utatAm /
   sa eva brahmaśabdārtho nārāyaṇapadoditaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.9 //	saH eva brahma-Sabda-arTaH nArAyaNa-pada-uditaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.9 //
   sa eva bhargaśabdārtho vyāhṛtīnāṃ ca bhūmataḥ /	saH eva Barga-Sabda-arTaH vyAhRtInAm ca BUmataH /
   bhāvanāccaiva sutvācca so 'yaṃ puruṣa ityapi // MAnuv_1,1.10 //	BAvanAt-ca-eva sutvAt-ca saH ayam puruzaH iti-api // Ma-anuv_1,1.10 //
   sa eva sarvavedārtho jijñāsyo 'yaṃ vidhīyate /	saH eva sarva-veda-arTaH jijQAsyaH ayam viDIyate /
   jñānī priyatamo 'to me taṃ vidvāneva cāmṛtaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.11 //	jQAnI priyatamaH atas me tam vidvAn-eva ca-amRtaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.11 //
   vṛṇute yaṃ tena labhya ityādyuktibalena hi /	vRNute yam tena laByaH ityAt-yukti-balena hi /
   jijñāsotthajñānajāt tatprasādādeva mucyate // MAnuv_1,1.12 //	jijQAsA-utTa-jQAna-jAt tad-prasAdAt-eva mucyate // Ma-anuv_1,1.12 //
   dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvo jīva eva ca /	dravyam karma ca kAlaH-ca svaBAvaH jIvaH eva ca /
   yadanugrahataḥ santi na santi yadupekṣayā // MAnuv_1,1.13 //	yat-anugrahataH santi na santi yat-upekzayA // Ma-anuv_1,1.13 //
   narte tvat kriyate kiñcidityāderna hariṃ vinā /	na-Rte tvat kriyate kiQcid-iti-AdeH-na harim vinA /
   jñānasvabhāvato 'pi syānmuktiḥ kasyāpi hi kvacit // MAnuv_1,1.14 //	jQAna-svaBAvataH api syAt-muktiH kasya-api hi kvacid // Ma-anuv_1,1.14 //
   ajñānāṃ jñānado viṣṇurjñānināṃ mokṣadaśca saḥ /	ajQAnAm jQAna-daH vizNuH-jQAninAm mokza-daH-ca saH /
   ānandadaśca muktānāṃ sa evaiko janārdanaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.15 //	Ananda-daH-ca muktAnAm saH eva-ekaH janArdanaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.15 //
   ityukterbandhamithyātvaṃ naiva muktirapekṣate /	iti-ukteH-banDa-miTyAtvam na-eva muktiH-apekzate /
   mithyātvamapi bandhasya na pratyakṣavirodhataḥ // MAnuv_1,1.16 //	miTyAtvam-api banDasya na pratyakza-viroDataH // Ma-anuv_1,1.16 //
   mithyātvaṃ yadi duḥkhādestadvākyāgrato bhavet /	miTyAtvam yadi duHKa-AdeH-tad-vAkya-agratas Bavet /
   mithyāyāḥ sādhakatvaṃ ca na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.17 //	miTyAyAH sADaka-tvam ca na sidDam prativAdinaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.17 //
   tacca mithyāpramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā /	tat-ca miTyA-pramANena satA vA sADyate tvayA /
   satā ced dvaitasiddhiḥ syānna siddhaṃ cānyasādhanam // MAnuv_1,1.18 //	satA ced dvEta-sidDiH syAt-na sidDam ca-anya-sADanam // Ma-anuv_1,1.18 //
   sādhakatvaṃ satastena sākṣiṇā siddhimicchatā /	sADaka-tvam sataH-tena sAkziNA sidDim-icCatA /
   svīkṛtaṃ hyaviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhakatā punaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.19 //	svIkRtam hi-aviSezasya sADyA sADaka-tA punar // Ma-anuv_1,1.19 //
   taccāviśeṣamānena sādhyamityanavasthitiḥ /	tat-ca-AviSeza-mAnena sADyam-iti-anavasTitiH /
   anaṅgīkurvatāṃ viśvasatyatāṃ tanna vāditā // MAnuv_1,1.20 //	anaFgIkurvatAm viSvasatyatAm tat-na vAditAH // Ma-anuv_1,1.20 //
   tasmād vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satyetyeva vyavasthitā /	tasmAt vyavahRtiH sarvA satya-iti-eva vyavasTitAH /
   vyāvahārikametasmāt satyamityeva cāgatam // MAnuv_1,1.21 //	vyAvahArikam-etasmAt satyam-iti-eva ca-Agatam // Ma-anuv_1,1.21 //
   vyavahārasataścāpi sādhakatvaṃ tu pūrvavat /	vyavahArasataH-ca-api sADaka-tvam tu pUrvavat /
   sattraividhyaṃ ca mānena siddhayet keneti pṛcchyate // MAnuv_1,1.22 //	sattrEviDyam ca mAnena sidDayet kena-iti pRcCyate // Ma-anuv_1,1.22 //
   tasyāpyuktaprakāreṇa naiva siddhiḥ kathañcana /	tasya-api-ukta-prakAreNa na-eva sidDiH kaTaQcana /
   vailakṣaṇyaṃ sadasatorapyetena niṣidhyate // MAnuv_1,1.23 //	vElakzaNyam sat-asatoH-api-etena niziDyate // Ma-anuv_1,1.23 //
   vailakṣaṇyaṃ sataścāpi svayaṃ sadbhedavādinaḥ /	vElakzaNyam sataH-ca-api svayam sat-Beda-vAdinaH /
   asataścāpi viśvasya tenāniṣyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet // MAnuv_1,1.24 //	asataH-ca-api viSvasya tena-anizyam kaTam Bavet // Ma-anuv_1,1.24 //
   yadyucyate 'pi sarvasmāditi sadbhedasaṃsthitiḥ /	yadi-ucyate api sarvasmAt-iti sadBeda-saMsTitiH /
   sanmātratvaṃ brahmaṇo 'pi tasmāt tadapi no bhavet // MAnuv_1,1.25 //	sat-mAtra-tvam brahmaNaH api tasmAt tat-api naH Bavet // Ma-anuv_1,1.25 //
   jñānabādhyatvamapi tu na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ /	jQAna-bADya-tvam-api tu na sidDam prativAdinaH /
   vijñātasyānyathā samyag vijñānaṃ hyeva tanmatam // MAnuv_1,1.26 //	vijQAtasya-anyaTA samyak vijQAnam hi-eva tat-matam // Ma-anuv_1,1.26 //
   asadvilakṣaṇajñaptyai jñātavyamasadeva hi /	asat-vilakzaNa-jQaptyE jQAtavyam-asat-eva hi /
   tasmādasatpratītiśca kathaṃ tena nivāryate // MAnuv_1,1.27 //	tasmAt-asat-pratItiH-ca kaTam tena nivAryate // Ma-anuv_1,1.27 //
   anyathātvamasat tasmād bhrāntāveva pratīyate /	anyaTAtvam-asat tasmAt BrAntO=-eva pratIyate /
   sattvasyāsata evaṃ hi svīkāryaiva pratītatā // MAnuv_1,1.28 //	sattvasya-asate evam hi svIkArya-eva pratIta-tA // Ma-anuv_1,1.28 //
   tasyānirvacanīyatve syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ /	tasya-anirvacanIya-tve syAt-eva hi-anavasTitiH /
   nirviśeṣe svayaṃ bhāte kimajñānāvṛtaṃ bhavetaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.29 //	nirviSeze svayam BAte kim-ajQAna-AvRtam BavetaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.29 //
   mithyāviśeṣo 'pyajñānasiddhimeva hyapekṣate /	miTyA-viSezaH api-ajQAna-sidDim-eva hi-apekzate /
   nacāavaraṇamajñānamasatye tena ceṣyate // MAnuv_1,1.30 //	nacAa-varaNam-ajQAnam-asatye tena ca-izyate // Ma-anuv_1,1.30 //
   aprakāśasvarūpatvājjaḍe 'jñānaṃ na manyate /	aprakASa-svarUpa-tvAt-jaxe ajQAnam na manyate /
   ajñānābhāvataḥ śāstraṃ sarvaṃ vyarthībhaviṣyati // MAnuv_1,1.31 //	ajQAna-aBAvataH SAstram sarvam vyarTIBavizyati // Ma-anuv_1,1.31 //
   ajñānasya ca mithyātvamajñānāditi kalpane /	ajQAnasya ca miTyAtvam-ajQAnAt-iti kalpane /

   avidyādurghaṭatvaṃ cet syādātmāpi hi tādṛśaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.33 //	avidyA-durGawa-tvam ced syAt-AtmA-api hi tAdRSaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.33 //

   na brahmatāṃ vaded vedo jīvasya hi kathañcana // MAnuv_1,1.35 //	na brahma-tAm vadet vedaH jIvasya hi kaTaQcana // Ma-anuv_1,1.35 //

   sārvajñyādiguṇaṃ jīvād bhinnaṃ jñāpayati śrutiḥ /	sArvajQi-Adi-guNam jIvAt Binnam jQApayati SrutiH /
   īśaṃ tāmupajīvyaiva vartate hyaikyavādinī // MAnuv_1,1.37 //	ISam tAm-upajIvya-eva vartate hi-Ekya-vAdinI // Ma-anuv_1,1.37 //
   upajīvyavirodhena nāsyāstanmānatā bhavet /	upajIvya-viroDena na-asya-aH-tat-mAnatA Bavet /
   svātantrye ca viśiṣṭatve sthānamattyaikyayorapi // MAnuv_1,1.38 //	svAtantrye ca viSizwa-tve sTAna-mattya-EkyayoH-api // Ma-anuv_1,1.38 //
   sādṛśye caikyavāk samyak sāvakāśā yatheṣyataḥ /	sAdRSye ca-Ekya-vAc samyak sa-avakASAH yaTA-izyataH /
   avakāśojkhitā bhedaśrutirnātibalā katham // MAnuv_1,1.39 //	avakASa-ujKitA Beda-SrutiH-na-ati-balA kaTam // Ma-anuv_1,1.39 //
   ajñānāsambhavādeva mithyābhedo nirākṛtaḥ /	ajQAna-asamBavAt-eva miTyA-BedaH nirAkRtaH /
   ato yathārthabandhasya vinā viṣṇuprasādataḥ // MAnuv_1,1.40 //	atas yaTA-arTa-banDasya vinA vizNu-prasAdataH // Ma-anuv_1,1.40 //
   anivṛttestadarthaṃ hi jijñāsātra vidhīyate /	anivRtteH-tad-arTam hi jijQAsA-atra viDIyate /
   yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandhāpanodakṛt // MAnuv_1,1.41 //	yaTA dRzwayA prasannaH san rAjA banDa-apanoda-kRt // Ma-anuv_1,1.41 //
   evaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryād bandhavibhedanam /	evam dRzwaH sa BagavAn kuryAt banDa-viBedanam /
   kāryatā ca na kācit syādiṣṭasādhanatāṃ vinā // MAnuv_1,1.42 //	kArya-tA ca na kAcid syAt-izwa-sADana-tAm vinA // Ma-anuv_1,1.42 //
   kāryaṃ na hi kriyāvyāpyaṃ niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ /	kAryam na hi kriyA-vyApyam nizidDasya samatvataH /
   na bhaviṣyatkriyā kāryaṃ srakṣyatīśa iti hyapi // MAnuv_1,1.43 //	na Bavizyat-kriyA kAryam srakzyati-ISaH iti hi-api // Ma-anuv_1,1.43 //
   kāryaṃ syānnaiva cākartumaśakyaṃ kāryamiṣyate /	kAryam syAt-na-eva ca-akartum-aSakyam kAryam-izyate /
   sāmyādeva niṣiddhasya tadiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ tathā // MAnuv_1,1.44 //	sAmyAt-eva nizidDasya tat-izwam sADanam taTA // Ma-anuv_1,1.44 //
   kāryaṃ sādhanamiṣṭasya bhagavāniṣṭadevatā /	kAryam sADanam-izwasya BagavAn-izwadevatA /
   mukhyeṣyaṃ vā sumanasāṃ preyastaditi ca śrutiḥ // MAnuv_1,1.45 //	muKyezyam vA sumanasAm preyaH-tat-iti ca SrutiH // Ma-anuv_1,1.45 //
   prāṇabuddhimanaḥkhātmadehāpatyadhanādayaḥ /	prANa-budDi-manaH-Ka-Atma-deha-apatya-Dana-AdayaH /
   yatsamparkāt priyā āsaṃstataḥ ko nvaparaḥ priyaḥ // MAnuv_1,1.46 //	yad-samparkAt priyAH Asan=-tatas kaH nu-aparaH priyaH // Ma-anuv_1,1.46 //
   ityādivākyairākāṅkṣāsannidhiryogyatā yataḥ /	ityAdi-vAkyEH-AkAFkzA-sanniDiH-yogya-tA yatas /
   asminneva samastasyetīṣye vyutpattiriṣyate // MAnuv_1,1.47 //	asmin=-eva samastasya-itIzye vyutpattiH-izyate // Ma-anuv_1,1.47 //
   attyapūpāṃstava bhrātetyādāvāvāpato 'pi ca /	attya-pUpAn=-tava BrAtA-iti-AdO=-O=-ApataH api ca /
   udvāpād vartamānatvādākāṅkṣādibalādapi // MAnuv_1,1.48 //	udvApAt vartamAna-tvAt-AkAFkza-Adi-balAt-api // Ma-anuv_1,1.48 //
   bālo vyutpattimapyeti nānayetyādivākyataḥ /	bAlaH vyutpattim-apyeti nAnayA-ityAdi-vAkyataH /
   ānīyamānadṛṣṭayaiva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati // MAnuv_1,1.49 //	AnIyamAna-dRzwayA-eva vyutpatteH samBave sati // Ma-anuv_1,1.49 //
   eṣyadānayanāyāyaṃ kuta eva pratīkṣate /	ezyat-AnayanAya-ayam kutas eva pratIkzate /
   vyutpanno vartamāne tu kriyāśabde bhaviṣyati // MAnuv_1,1.50 //	vyutpannaH vartamAne tu kriyA-Sabde Bavizyati // Ma-anuv_1,1.50 //
   punardṛṣṭyaiva śabdaśrut paścāt vyutpattimeṣyati /	punar-dRzwyA-eva Sabda-SruD paScAt vyutpattim-ezyati /
   vartamānamatītaṃ ca bhaviṣyaditi ca kramāt // MAnuv_1,1.51 //	vartamAnam-atItam ca Bavizyat-iti ca kramAt // Ma-anuv_1,1.51 //
   ākāṅkṣādiyutaṃ yasmād vidhervyutpādanaṃ kutaḥ /	AkAFkza-Adi-yutam yasmAt viDeH-vyutpAdanam kutas /
   dṛṣṭyā jñātapadārthasya padākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati // MAnuv_1,1.52 //	dRzwyA jQAta-padArTasya pada-AkAFkzA Bavizyati // Ma-anuv_1,1.52 //
   vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmād vatarmāne gate tataḥ /	vyutpattiH praTamA tasmAt vatarmAne gate tatas /
   iṣṭamākāṅkṣate sarvo na pravṛttimapekṣate // MAnuv_1,1.53 //	izwam-AkAFkzate sarvaH na pravRttim-apekzate // Ma-anuv_1,1.53 //
   aparokṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā jñānamiṣṭasya sādhanam /	aparokzam parokzam vA jQAnam-izwasya sADanam /
   kvāpi ceṣyā tadarthā syādattirhi rasavittaye // MAnuv_1,1.54 //	kvApi cezyA tad-arTA syAt-attiH-hi rasa-vittaye // Ma-anuv_1,1.54 //
   vākyārthajñānamātreṇa kvacidiṣṭaṃ bhavedapi /	vAkya-arTa-jQAna-mAtreNa kvacid-izwam Bavet-api /
   na ca srukasruvavahnayādāvatātparyaṃ śruterbhavet // MAnuv_1,1.55 //	na ca srukasruva-vahnayA-adAvatAt-paryam SruteH-Bavet // Ma-anuv_1,1.55 //
   yatkiñcitkaraṇarasyāpi yajñataivānyathā bhavet /	yat-kiQcit-karaNa-rasya-api yajQa-tA-eva-anyaTA Bavet /
   tasmādupāsanārthaṃ ca svārthe tātparyavad bhavet // MAnuv_1,1.56 //	tasmAt-upAsana-arTam ca sva-arTe tAtparyavat Bavet // Ma-anuv_1,1.56 //
   iti śabdonnaye 'gnāvityunnīte smṛtirbhavet /	iti Sabda-unnaye agnO=-iti-unnIte smRtiH-Bavet /
   itiśabdavyapetāni hyapi santi vacāṃsyalam // MAnuv_1,1.57 //	iti-Sabda-vyapetAni hi-api santi vacAMsi-alam // Ma-anuv_1,1.57 //
   ātmānamevetyādīni yoge 'gnāvapi tat samam /	AtmAnam-eva-ityAdIni yoge agnO=-api tat samam /
   ekavākyatvayoge tu vedasyāpi hyaśeṣataḥ // MAnuv_1,1.58 //	eka-vAkya-tva-yoge tu vedasya-api hi-aSezatas // Ma-anuv_1,1.58 //
   vākyabhedo na yuktaḥ syād yogaśca syānmahāphale /	vAkya-BedaH na yuktaH syAt yogaH-ca syAt-mahA-Pale /
   iti brūyāditi vaco gatamagnau samīpagam // MAnuv_1,1.59 //	iti brUyAt-iti vacaH gatam-agnO samIpa-gam // Ma-anuv_1,1.59 //
   kalpanāgauravaṃ cet syāt pṛthak tātparyasambhave /	kalpanA-gOravam ced syAt pRTak tAtparya-samBave /
   kalpanāgauravādeva padārthā na syureva hi // MAnuv_1,1.60 //	kalpanA-gOravAt-eva padArTAH na syuH-eva hi // Ma-anuv_1,1.60 //
